The gadgets are several practical applications (compass, movement security systems - door or luggage security, magnetic security system, accelerometer mouse, remote control for PC and wireless presenters for PowerPoint) that use one or more sensors from a specific SensorTag to achieve a concrete, fully functional and useful application.\r\n\r\n3. can trigger a visual or/and an audible warning or/and a data saving process will be started if an event will be generated - if the desired value (instantaneous, mean or variance), of a specific sensor, meet a condition or a series of conditions (is lower, higher, inside or outside of a specific range);\r\n\r\n4. using the activities feature, the blessTags application will execute different actions, when a specific event will take place.
